msg:I stayed in Xiamen for seven nights and this was the best value for money among all the five-star hotels I stayed in. Less than 700, including breakfast, welcome fruits, tickets to Chengyi Science and Technology Discovery Center, and sandwich energy packs.

But it can also be clearly felt that this is an old five-star hotel. Compared with those newly built in recent years, the room equipment is slightly outdated, the toilet is not smart, the room is equipped with instant coffee, and the toiletries are of average quality.

The most praiseworthy thing is the breakfast, which is rich in variety. There is much more variety than the other ones I have stayed at. The light buffet at 88 in the evening is also very cost-effective.

Some of the rules are a bit rigid. For example, when I ordered it, there was no robot outside, only the front desk staff delivered it, and they signed a food exemption agreement; I asked the guest room staff for a bath bag for the bathtub, but he hesitated and said there was no one, so I asked the front desk, and I only knew the fee after asking the front desk. Can't you just tell me the fee? But I don‚Äôt understand why there is no bath bag in the bathtub? Five-star hotels in Siming District not only provide bath bags, but also bubble baths and rose baths for free to customers.
